             </noscript>
            </a>
            M
            <br/>
            <a href="/wiki/Computer_Software_Rating_Regulation" title="Computer Software Rating Regulation">
             CSRR
            </a>
            :Yellow
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td class="seriesa" style="white-space:nowrap">
            <b>
             Platforms
            </b>
           </td>
           <td class="seriesb" style="border: 1px black solid;">
            <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_3" title="PlayStation 3">
             PlayStation 3
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="/wiki/Xbox_360" title="Xbox 360">
             Xbox 360
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" title="Microsoft Windows">
             Microsoft Windows
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="/wiki/Steam" title="Steam">
             Steam
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="/wiki/IOS" title="IOS">
             iOS
            </a>
            &amp;
            <a href="/wiki/Android_(System)" title="Android (System)">
             Android
            </a>
            via
            <a href="/wiki/Dive_In" title="Dive In">
             Dive In
            </a>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <q>
            The future belongs not to those who wait...
           </q>
          </dd>
          <dd>
           
           <i>
            Final Fantasy XIII
           </i>
           Game Trailer
          </dd>
          <dd>
           <q>
            The Battle Within Begins...
           </q>
          </dd>
          <dd>
           
           <i>
            Final Fantasy XIII
           </i>
           tagline
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          <i>
           <b>
            Final Fantasy XIII
           </b>
          </i>
          is the thirteenth installment in the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_(Series)" title="Final Fantasy (Series)">
            Final Fantasy
           </a>
          </i>
          main series, and is the first of the series to be released on the
          <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_3" title="PlayStation 3">
           PlayStation 3
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Xbox_360" title="Xbox 360">
           Xbox 360
          </a>
          . Unveiled at E3 2006, the game is the flagship of
          <a href="/wiki/Square_Enix" title="Square Enix">
           Square Enix
          </a>
          's
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Fabula_Nova_Crystallis:_Final_Fantasy" title="Fabula Nova Crystallis: Final Fantasy">
            Fabula Nova Crystallis
           </a>
          </i>
          project. The game runs on
          <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Tools" title="Crystal Tools">
           Crystal Tools
          </a>
          , a proprietary engine built for Square Enix's seventh generation games.
         </p>
         <p>
          The game was released in Japan on December 17, 2009, and March 9, 2010 for North America and Europe. A traditional Chinese version for PlayStation 3 was released in May 27, 2010
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">
           <a href="#cite_note-2">
            [3]
           </a>
          </sup>
          .
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XIII
          </i>
          is the first
          <i>
           Final Fantasy
          </i>
          game translated into traditional Chinese. A sequel titled
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII-2" title="Final Fantasy XIII-2">
            Final Fantasy XIII-2
           </a>
          </i>
          was released on December 15th, 2011, and a second sequel,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Lightning_Returns:_Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Lightning Returns: Final Fantasy XIII">
            Lightning Returns: Final Fantasy XIII
           </a>
          </i>
          , was announced on September 1st, 2012, and released in 2014.
         </p>
         <nav class="toc" id="toc">
          <div id="toctitle">
           <h2>
            Contents
           </h2>
           <span class="toctoggle">
            [
            <a class="internal" data-hide="hide" data-show="show" href="#" id="togglelink">
             show
            </a>
            ]
           </span>
          </div>
          <ol>
          </ol>
         </nav>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Gameplay">
           Gameplay
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit Gameplay section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141205165639/finalfantasy/images/3/38/Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png">
           <img alt="Archylte Steppe Enemies" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png" data-image-name="Archylte Steppe Enemies.png" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141205165639/finalfantasy/images/thumb/3/38/Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png/180px-Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Archylte Steppe Enemies" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png" data-image-name="Archylte Steppe Enemies.png" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141205165639/finalfantasy/images/thumb/3/38/Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png/180px-Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Archylte_Steppe_Enemies.png">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Player traveling the field map with multiple enemies in sight.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The game's progression is
          <a href="/wiki/Chapter" title="Chapter">
           chapter
          </a>
          -based and in most chapters, the player will see the story through different characters' view. Players can move around the field map while controlling the
          <a href="/wiki/Party" title="Party">
           party
          </a>
          leader, the other members moving independently, sometimes running ahead, engaging in dialogue, or stopping to look at objects on the field and pointing things of interest out to the party leader. Other party members being far away from the leader does not affect their participation in
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_(Term)" title="Battle (Term)">
           battles
          </a>
          that take place in a separate module. Players can jump, but only at specific jump spots marked on the map.
         </p>
         <p>
          Enemies will appear on the map and battles initiate when coming into contact with them. Treasure chests cannot be opened in close proximity to a monster, and there are several instances enemies are "guarding" treasures and must be banished to collect the loot.
          <a href="/wiki/Shroud" title="Shroud">
           Shrouds
          </a>
          can be used to move about the field without triggering enemy encounters, and to bestow the party with buffs prior to the battle's start.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20150119165827/finalfantasy/images/4/4a/FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png">
           <img alt="FFXIII Three Way Battle" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png" data-image-name="FFXIII Three Way Battle.png" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20150119165827/finalfantasy/images/thumb/4/4a/FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png/180px-FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="FFXIII Three Way Battle" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png" data-image-name="FFXIII Three Way Battle.png" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20150119165827/finalfantasy/images/thumb/4/4a/FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png/180px-FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:FFXIII_Three_Way_Battle.png">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Three way battle between Behemoth King, Megistotherian, and the party.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Some enemies on the map may fight against each other and if the player contacts them it will start a three way battle.
         </p>
         <p>
          Players can't set the party or the party leader until later into the game, diversity being brought in via the
          <a href="#Paradigm_Shift">
           Paradigm Shift
          </a>
          system. If the party leader is incapacitated in battle, it will result in a
          <a href="/wiki/Game_Over_(Term)" title="Game Over (Term)">
           Game Over
          </a>
          , but if a battle ends in defeat, the player will simply appear in the point on the field right before the fight was initiated, and they may either re-attempt the battle or leave it.
         </p>
         <p>
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XIII
          </i>
          is the third main series
          <i>
           Final Fantasy
          </i>
          game in which the player does not routinely win
          <a href="/wiki/Gil" title="Gil">
           gil
          </a>
          from battles; rather the player obtains the currency from
          <a href="/wiki/Treasure_Chest_(Object)" title="Treasure Chest (Object)">
           treasure spheres
          </a>
          , or from selling items. The first such game was
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_VIII" title="Final Fantasy VIII">
            Final Fantasy VIII
           </a>
          </i>
          , where gil was received as
          <a href="/wiki/SeeD" title="SeeD">
           SeeD
          </a>
          salary, and the second was
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XII" title="Final Fantasy XII">
            Final Fantasy XII
           </a>
          </i>
          , where although it is possible for some defeated enemies to drop gil, it is not a universal reward for victory.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Save_Point" title="Save Point">
           Save Stations
          </a>
          allow the player not only to save, but access the shops in
          <a href="/wiki/Retail_Network" title="Retail Network">
           Retail Network
          </a>
          where items can be bought or sold.
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Command_Synergy_Battle">
           Command Synergy Battle
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit Command Synergy Battle section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100109225454/finalfantasy/images/2/25/FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg">
           <img alt="FFXIII-English Fang Battle" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg" data-image-name="FFXIII-English Fang Battle.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100109225454/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/25/FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg/180px-FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="FFXIII-English Fang Battle" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg" data-image-name="FFXIII-English Fang Battle.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100109225454/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/25/FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg/180px-FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:FFXIII-English_Fang_Battle.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Combat in
            <i>
             Final Fantasy XIII
            </i>
            , showing
            <a href="/wiki/Oerba_Yun_Fang" title="Oerba Yun Fang">
             Fang
            </a>
            attacking an enemy.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/Command_Synergy_Battle" title="Command Synergy Battle">
             Command Synergy Battle
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          The
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_System" title="Battle System">
           battle system
          </a>
          , called Command Synergy Battle in-game, has been described as "more tactical than
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_X" title="Final Fantasy X">
            Final Fantasy X
           </a>
          </i>
          , faster than
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_X-2" title="Final Fantasy X-2">
            Final Fantasy X-2
           </a>
          </i>
          , and almost as seamless as
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XII" title="Final Fantasy XII">
            Final Fantasy XII
           </a>
          </i>
          ". The enemies are visible in the field. When the player runs into them, the screen lights up and the scene switches to a vast, blank battlefield, marking the start of a battle where the player can control one character out of a party of up to three. After a certain point in the game the lead character can be switched.
         </p>
         <p>
          The
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_System#Active_Time_Battle" title="Battle System">
           Active Time Battle
          </a>
          gauge is divided into sections. Each command has a numeric value referred to as "ATB Cost" next to the name indicating how many of these sections it will take up. This allows the player to input several commands per turn. The next turn comes up sooner if the ATB bar is only partially used.
          <a href="/wiki/Magic_(Command)#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Magic (Command)">
           Magic
          </a>
          and summoning are only available to party members who are
          <a href="/wiki/L%27Cie" title="L'Cie">
           l'Cie
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          A new element called the
          <a href="/wiki/Stagger" title="Stagger">
           Chain Gauge
          </a>
          is specific to each enemy, and fills as the player performs attack combos marked by a percentage. Upon filling the gauge the enemy enters "Stagger Mode", where even more damage can be done. Staggered enemies can be launched in the air and juggled with attacks. Staggering is almost essential to winning many battles.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722041142/finalfantasy/images/5/5e/Battle_Results_FFXIII.png">
           <img alt="Battle Results FFXIII" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Battle_Results_FFXIII.png" data-image-name="Battle Results FFXIII.png" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722041142/finalfantasy/images/thumb/5/5e/Battle_Results_FFXIII.png/180px-Battle_Results_FFXIII.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Battle Results FFXIII" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Battle_Results_FFXIII.png" data-image-name="Battle Results FFXIII.png" height="101" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722041142/finalfantasy/images/thumb/5/5e/Battle_Results_FFXIII.png/180px-Battle_Results_FFXIII.png" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Battle_Results_FFXIII.png">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            A Battle Result in
            <i>
             Final Fantasy XIII
            </i>
            .
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Because of the ATB cost determining the moves a player can use, there is no
          <a href="/wiki/MP_(Stat)" title="MP (Stat)">
           MP
          </a>
          in the game. Since magic cannot be used outside of battle, the party's
          <a href="/wiki/HP_(Stat)" title="HP (Stat)">
           HP
          </a>
          is restored after every battle.
          <a href="/wiki/Full_ATB_Skill" title="Full ATB Skill">
           Full ATB Skills
          </a>
          work similar to
          <a href="/wiki/Limit_Break_(Ability)" title="Limit Break (Ability)">
           Limit Breaks
          </a>
          from previous games as being character-specific special moves and even if there is no
          <a href="/wiki/Escape_(Command)" title="Escape (Command)">
           Escape
          </a>
          command, the player can leave battle with the Retry option.
         </p>
         <p>
          When a battle is won, a
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_Results" title="Battle Results">
           Battle Results
          </a>
          screen pops up, giving the player a zero-to-five stars ranking on how they did, as well as showing how long the battle took. This information is linked to the
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Achievements_and_Trophies" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Achievements and Trophies">
           Trophy and Achievement systems
          </a>
          .
          <br style="clear:both"/>
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Paradigm_Shift">
           Paradigm Shift
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit Paradigm Shift section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150803/finalfantasy/images/e/ed/Paradigm_shift.jpg">
           <img alt="Paradigm shift" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Paradigm_shift.jpg" data-image-name="Paradigm shift.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150803/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/ed/Paradigm_shift.jpg/180px-Paradigm_shift.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Paradigm shift" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Paradigm_shift.jpg" data-image-name="Paradigm shift.jpg" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150803/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/ed/Paradigm_shift.jpg/180px-Paradigm_shift.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Paradigm_shift.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The Paradigm Shift system.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/Paradigm" title="Paradigm">
             Paradigm
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          The player can only control one character at a time in battle. The other party members' actions are governed by a system called the "Paradigm Shift". Paradigms are described as "stances" or "classes" the characters temporarily take during battle to define the abilities they use. They are more strict than
          <a href="/wiki/Job_System" title="Job System">
           job classes
          </a>
          ; for example, the party member with a
          <a href="/wiki/Medic_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Medic (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Medic
          </a>
          's role can do nothing but heal, while the
          <a href="/wiki/Commando_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Commando (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Commando's
          </a>
          role forces them to only attack with non-elemental attacks.
         </p>
         <p>
          The paradigms can be changed at any time to suit the situation at hand, but they cannot be changed individually, only for the whole party at a time. Thus, a paradigm is a combination of three roles. There are a total of 83 possible paradigm combinations (6 single, 21 double, and 56 triple member combinations). The roles used are shown as colored abbreviations next to the characters' names in the battle screen.
         </p>
         <p>
          The roles within the paradigms are:
         </p>
         <table class="full-width FFXIII table">
          <tr class="a">
           <th style="width: 20%;">
            Role
           </th>
           <th style="width: 10%;">
            Color
           </th>
           <th style="width: 50%;">
            Description
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Commando_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Commando (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Commando
            </a>
            (COM)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Attacker (ATK)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="red">
           </td>
           <td>
            Build attack chains more easily with enhanced strength.
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Ravager_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Ravager (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Ravager
            </a>
            (RAV)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Blaster (BLA)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="blue">
           </td>
           <td>
            Charge enemy chain gauges with concentrated attacks.
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Sentinel_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Sentinel (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Sentinel
            </a>
            (SEN)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Defender (DEF)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="gold">
           </td>
           <td>
            Shield allies from enemy attacks.
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Saboteur_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Saboteur (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Saboteur
            </a>
            (SAB)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Jammer (JAM)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="gray">
           </td>
           <td>
            Enfeeble enemies while charging their chain gauges.
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Synergist_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Synergist (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Synergist
            </a>
            (SYN)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Enhancer (ENH)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="purple">
           </td>
           <td>
            Support allies with an array of magical enhancements.
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <th class="b">
            <a href="/wiki/Medic_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Medic (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Medic
            </a>
            (MED)
            <br/>
            (
            <abbr class="footnote" style="">
             Healer (HLR)
             <span style="display:none">
              Name in Japanese: 
             </span>
            </abbr>
            )
           </th>
           <td bgcolor="green">
           </td>
           <td>
            Focus on restoring HP and removing
            <a href="/wiki/Status_Effect" title="Status Effect">
             status ailments
            </a>
            .
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Crystarium">
           Crystarium
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit Crystarium section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150746/finalfantasy/images/2/27/Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg">
           <img alt="Hope&#039;s crystarium" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg" data-image-name="Hope's crystarium.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150746/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/27/Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg/180px-Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Hope&#039;s crystarium" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg" data-image-name="Hope's crystarium.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100824150746/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/27/Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg/180px-Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Hope%27s_crystarium.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Hope's Crystarium.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/Crystarium_System" title="Crystarium System">
             Crystarium System
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          Characters grow in power in a system similar to the
          <a href="/wiki/Sphere_Grid" title="Sphere Grid">
           Sphere Grid
          </a>
          from
          <i>
           Final Fantasy X
          </i>
          called the Crystarium System. Characters win "
          <a href="/wiki/Ability_Points" title="Ability Points">
           Crystogen Points
          </a>
          " (CP) in battle, and can use them to purchase
          <a href="/wiki/Stat_Growth" title="Stat Growth">
           stat boosts
          </a>
          , spells and other abilities on a circular chart. The skills a character learns affects their ability to learn other skills and opens new paths on the chart  learning
          <a href="/wiki/Fire_(Ability)" title="Fire (Ability)">
           Fire
          </a>
          , for example, opens a skill path that leads to
          <a href="/wiki/Fira_(Ability)" title="Fira (Ability)">
           Fira
          </a>
          and other spells.
         </p>
         <p>
          The available abilities in the Crystaria vary between party members, but series staples such as
          <a href="/wiki/Attack_(Command)" title="Attack (Command)">
           Attack
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Fire_(Ability)" title="Fire (Ability)">
           Fire
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Blizzard_(Ability)" title="Blizzard (Ability)">
           Blizzard
          </a>
          , and
          <a href="/wiki/Cure_(Ability)" title="Cure (Ability)">
           Cure
          </a>
          make a return, along with new commands such as
          <a href="/wiki/Blitz_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Blitz (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Blitz
          </a>
          , which causes area-of-effect damage, and
          <a href="/wiki/Ruin_(Ability)" title="Ruin (Ability)">
           Ruin
          </a>
          , a new
          <a href="/wiki/Non-elemental" title="Non-elemental">
           non-elemental
          </a>
          spell.
         </p>
         <p>
          The system opens up in stages, and party members cannot develop further after reaching the end of the current stage. The final stage of the Crystarium is only opened by defeating the final boss, meaning to fully develop the party players must take on the post-game content.
          <br style="clear:both"/>
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Equipment">
           Equipment
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit Equipment section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722040208/finalfantasy/images/2/26/Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg">
           <img alt="Ffxiii status screen" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg" data-image-name="Ffxiii status screen.jpg" data-src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722040208/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/26/Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg/180px-Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Ffxiii status screen" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg" data-image-name="Ffxiii status screen.jpg" height="101" src="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722040208/finalfantasy/images/thumb/2/26/Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg/180px-Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Ffxiii_status_screen.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Lightning's status screen.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Each character has eight unique base
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Weapons" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Weapons">
           weapons
          </a>
          , most of which can be found in the game, and all of which can be purchased at Retail Network stores. The base weapons can be upgraded to a unique second stage, and eventually to its third and ultimate stage. The third stage of all the weapons of a particular character share a common name, but have different stats and abilities depending upon which weapon it was upgraded from.
         </p>
         <p>
          All characters can equip all
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Accessories" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Accessories">
           accessories
          </a>
          . Each character can initially equip one accessory at a time, but this capacity can be increased to up to four through upgrades obtained in the characters' Crystaria.
         </p>
         <p>
          In addition to the basic
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Passive_Abilities" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Passive Abilities">
           enhancements
          </a>
          provided by weapons and accessories, when a character equips weapons and accessories that belong to the same "
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Passive_Abilities#Synthesis_Abilities" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Passive Abilities">
           synthesis
          </a>
          " group (a hidden property), the character can gain additional passive enhancements (such as increased ATB gauge recharge rate).
         </p>
         <p>
          The basic enhancements weapons and accessories grant to characters can also increase as the items are upgraded through the application of various
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Components" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Components">
           components
          </a>
          to increase its Experience Points (EXP). When the weapon or accessory reaches a certain number of EXP, it will be upgraded to a new "level". Once it reaches a certain level (usually 25 for weapons and 2 to 5 for equipment), the number will be replaced by a star (), at which point it can no longer be upgraded by standard components. It can however be
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Upgrades" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Upgrades">
           transformed
          </a>
          with a stone ore
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Components#Catalysts" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Components">
           catalyst
          </a>
          into a new stage of the same class of equipment, with a new name, that can then continue to be levelled up for higher bonuses, although there are some accessories that transform into an item of a completely different synthesis group.
         </p>
         <p>
          There are three types of components: biological, mechanical and monetary. Biological components are dropped by biological enemies and although they don't generally have a high EXP value, they do increase the EXP bonus of the weapon or accessory, meaning that subsequent components will give up to 300% more EXP points compared to their base value. Mechanical components are dropped by mechanical enemies, and work in the opposite way to biological components, giving a high number of EXP points, at the expense of reducing the EXP bonus. Therefore, biological components should be used to build up the EXP bonus, before using mechanical components to add EXP. The final type is monetary components. These are dropped by human enemies, and although they have a nominal EXP value, they are intended to be sold for gil at shops to buy other, more effective components.
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Summoning">
           Summoning
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit Summoning section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722044027/finalfantasy/images/9/9c/Bahamut_summoned.jpg">
           <img alt="Bahamut summoned" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Bahamut_summoned.jpg" data-image-name="Bahamut summoned.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722044027/finalfantasy/images/thumb/9/9c/Bahamut_summoned.jpg/180px-Bahamut_summoned.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Bahamut summoned" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Bahamut_summoned.jpg" data-image-name="Bahamut summoned.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20100722044027/finalfantasy/images/thumb/9/9c/Bahamut_summoned.jpg/180px-Bahamut_summoned.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Bahamut_summoned.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Bahamut summoned to battle.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/Eidolon_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Eidolon (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Eidolon (Final Fantasy XIII)
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Summoned_Monsters" title="Summoned Monsters">
           Summons
          </a>
          return as Eidolons, linked with the powers of the
          <a href="/wiki/L%27Cie" title="L'Cie">
           l'Cie
          </a>
          . Playable Eidolons include the
          <a href="/wiki/Shiva#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Shiva">
           Shiva Sisters
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Odin#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Odin">
           Odin
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Bahamut#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Bahamut">
           Bahamut
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Alexander_(Summon)#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Alexander (Summon)">
           Alexander
          </a>
          , and two new summons,
          <a href="/wiki/Brynhildr_(Summon)" title="Brynhildr (Summon)">
           Brynhildr
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Hecatoncheir_(Summon)" title="Hecatoncheir (Summon)">
           Hecatoncheir
          </a>
          . While
          <a href="/wiki/Ifrit#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Ifrit">
           Ifrit
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Carbuncle_(Summon)#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Carbuncle (Summon)">
           Carbuncle
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Valefor_(Summon)#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Valefor (Summon)">
           Valefor
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Ramuh#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Ramuh">
           Ramuh
          </a>
          , and
          <a href="/wiki/Siren_(Summon)#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Siren (Summon)">
           Siren
          </a>
          make an appearance, they are not playable.
         </p>
         <p>
          The playable Eidolons have mechanical designs and the power to transform. The Eidolons are used both as a gameplay feature and as plot devices. Each character has one Eidolon, and Eidolons replace the other party members besides the summoner when called.
         </p>
         <p>
          Eidolons are summoned by the use of
          <a href="/wiki/Technical_Points" title="Technical Points">
           Technical Points
          </a>
          (TP), which are won after battles. Instead of HP, Eidolons use "Summon Points" (SP) to indicate their health, but SP also decreases over time. Once SP is depleted, the Eidolon will disappear, and the other party members will return. Each l'Cie must win the "approval" of their respective Eidolon by defeating them in combat.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130808015238/finalfantasy/images/b/bb/Ff13-odingestalt.jpg">
           <img alt="Ff13-odingestalt" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" data-image-name="Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130808015238/finalfantasy/images/thumb/b/bb/Ff13-odingestalt.jpg/180px-Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Ff13-odingestalt" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" data-image-name="Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" height="101" src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130808015238/finalfantasy/images/thumb/b/bb/Ff13-odingestalt.jpg/180px-Ff13-odingestalt.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Ff13-odingestalt.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Lightning and Odin's Gestalt Mode.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In addition to summoning Eidolons to fight alongside them, each Eidolon can transform into a form the summoner can ride in a mode called "
          <a href="/wiki/Eidolon_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)#Gestalt_Mode_by_Eidolon" title="Eidolon (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Gestalt Mode
          </a>
          " ("Driving Mode" in the Japanese version), where combat becomes more action-oriented, with the summon being able to perform various special attacks with certain button combinations.
         </p>
         <p>
          Each Eidolon's Gestalt Mode includes a powerful finisher move that will end the summoning. The duration of Gestalt Mode is determined by the Gestalt Gauge that appears once an Eidolon is summoned; the gauge will fill as the summoner builds attack chains with their Eidolon.
          <br style="clear:both"/>
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Missions">
           Missions
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit Missions section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/Missions_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Missions (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Missions (Final Fantasy XIII)
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130807232240/finalfantasy/images/e/e4/Cie%27th_stone.jpg">
           <img alt="Cie&#039;th stone" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Cie%27th_stone.jpg" data-image-name="Cie'th stone.jpg" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130807232240/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/e4/Cie%27th_stone.jpg/180px-Cie%27th_stone.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Cie&#039;th stone" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Cie%27th_stone.jpg" data-image-name="Cie'th stone.jpg" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130807232240/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/e4/Cie%27th_stone.jpg/180px-Cie%27th_stone.jpg" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Cie%27th_stone.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Missions are accepted from Cie'th Stones.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Gran_Pulse" title="Gran Pulse">
           Gran Pulse
          </a>
          has several points marked with
          <a href="/wiki/Cie%27th_Stone" title="Cie'th Stone">
           Cie'th Stones
          </a>
          where the party may acquire missions. These are similar in function to the
          <a href="/wiki/Hunt_(Final_Fantasy_XII)" title="Hunt (Final Fantasy XII)">
           Hunts
          </a>
          in
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XII
          </i>
          , and involve battling one of the many
          <a href="/wiki/Monster_(Term)" title="Monster (Term)">
           monsters
          </a>
          around Gran Pulse. They are not part of the main story, but players can experience
          <a href="/wiki/Focus_(Fabula_Nova_Crystallis)" title="Focus (Fabula Nova Crystallis)">
           Foci
          </a>
          of past l'Cie who failed to complete their assignments, and thus their targets are still alive. It is up to the player whether to defeat the specified enemy, some of which have been compared by the staff to mountains towering above the party e.g.:
          <a href="/wiki/Adamantoise_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Adamantoise (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Adamantoises
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          By completing these tasks the party can gain materials and items to improve their equipment. The main difference between the hunts of
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XII
          </i>
          and the missions of
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XIII
          </i>
          is that while every hunt can only be completed once, the player may take up each mission multiple times, although the mission reward can be obtained only once; subsequent missions will earn the player a different type of reward, usually of lesser quality (e.g.:
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Components#Bomb_Ashes" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Components">
           Bomb Ashes
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Components#Bomb_Shells" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Components">
           Bomb Shells
          </a>
          ). Replaying these missions is a requirement for those seeking to attain
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Achievements_and_Trophies" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Achievements and Trophies">
           all Achievements or Trophies
          </a>
          for the game, as one requires a 5-star battle rating earned for all missions.
         </p>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Setting">
           Setting
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit Setting section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130325094207/finalfantasy/images/8/88/Coccon_Exterior.png">
           <img alt="Coccon Exterior" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Coccon_Exterior.png" data-image-name="Coccon Exterior.png" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130325094207/finalfantasy/images/thumb/8/88/Coccon_Exterior.png/180px-Coccon_Exterior.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Coccon Exterior" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Coccon_Exterior.png" data-image-name="Coccon Exterior.png" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130325094207/finalfantasy/images/thumb/8/88/Coccon_Exterior.png/180px-Coccon_Exterior.png" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Coccon_Exterior.png">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Cocoon.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            See also:
            <a href="/wiki/Cocoon_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Cocoon (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Cocoon (Final Fantasy XIII)
            </a>
            and
            <a href="/wiki/Gran_Pulse" title="Gran Pulse">
             Gran Pulse
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
          <dd>
           <q>
            Cocoona utopia in the sky.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Its inhabitants believed their world a paradise. Under the Sanctum's rule, Cocoon had long known peace and prosperity.
            <br/>
            Mankind was blessed by its protectors, the benevolent fal'Cie, and believed that tranquil days would continue forever.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Their tranquility was shattered with the discovery of one hostile fal'Cie.
            <br/>
            The moment that fal'Cie from Pulsethe feared and detested lowerworldawoke from its slumber, peace on Cocoon came to an end.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Fal'Cie curse humans, turning them into magic-wielding servants. They become l'Ciechosen of the fal'Cie.
            <br/>
            Those branded with the mark of a l'Cie carry the burden of either fulfilling their Focus or facing a fate harsher than death itself.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            A prayer for redemption. A wish to protect the world. A promise to challenge destiny.
            <br/>
            After thirteen days of fates intertwined,
            <b>
             the battle begins.
            </b>
           </q>
          </dd>
          <dd>
           Official Prologue
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          Cocoon is a hollow floating world created thirteen centuries ago by the
          <a href="/wiki/Divinity_in_Final_Fantasy" title="Divinity in Final Fantasy">
           deity
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Lindzei" title="Lindzei">
           Lindzei
          </a>
          , and is ruled by fal'Cie; godlike beings of immense power and authority. Located in Gran Pulse's atmosphere, Cocoon is a futuristic utopian world isolated from the wilderness of the lowerworld. Cities exist on the inside of Cocoon's shell with barriers all around, and the people are forbidden to leave Cocoon. Machines and mechanized beasts are commissioned as the guardians of the citizens while the resident fal'Cie provide them with whatever they need from food and water to protection and guidance and entertainment. The people of Cocoon are conditioned to believe that Pulsians are savages out to destroy them and their paradise, and that Pulse is a world full of unknown terrors, a hell for humans.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120730162318/finalfantasy/images/3/3a/Vanille_Pulse.png">
           <img alt="Vanille Pulse" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Vanille_Pulse.png" data-image-name="Vanille Pulse.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120730162318/finalfantasy/images/thumb/3/3a/Vanille_Pulse.png/180px-Vanille_Pulse.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Vanille Pulse" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Vanille_Pulse.png" data-image-name="Vanille Pulse.png" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120730162318/finalfantasy/images/thumb/3/3a/Vanille_Pulse.png/180px-Vanille_Pulse.png" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Vanille_Pulse.png">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Gran Pulse with Cocoon floating above it.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Gran Pulse, known to the people of Cocoon simply as Pulse, is the expansive lowerworld beneath Cocoon, created by its namesake deity
          <a href="/wiki/Pulse" title="Pulse">
           Pulse
          </a>
          . As opposed to the Cocoon fal'Cie, Pulse fal'Cie only serve to cultivate the land, having little to do with human affairs. The plants and wildlife can evolve and grow to immense sizes, and the world is ruled by
          <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/natural_selection" title="wikipedia:natural selection">
           natural selection
          </a>
          where only the strongest survive. Compared to Cocoon, Gran Pulse is primitive with ancient technology and monsters roaming everywhere. The people of Pulse were raised to believe that Cocoon was a source of evil, a 'floating nest of vipers' posed to attack at any time.
         </p>
         <p>
          Six centuries ago, tensions between Cocoon and Gran Pulse rose to the point of war and the
          <a href="/wiki/War_of_Transgression" title="War of Transgression">
           War of Transgression
          </a>
          broke out. Two Pulsian girls were made l'Cie and bestowed with the power to transform into the legendary beast called
          <a href="/wiki/Ragnarok_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Ragnarok (Final Fantasy XIII)">
           Ragnarok
          </a>
          to destroy Cocoon. In the war's climax, Ragnarok cracked Cocoon's shell but failed to destroy the floating world. Cocoon was victorious and most of Gran Pulse's population had been wiped out. Cocoon's fal'Cie raided Pulse for raw materials to repair the damage sustained, and the war served to strengthen the people's paranoia towards Pulse.
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Characters">
           Characters
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit Characters section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111031122945/finalfantasy/images/e/e0/FFXIII_Characters.jpg">
           <img alt="FFXIII Characters" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="FFXIII_Characters.jpg" data-image-name="FFXIII Characters.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111031122945/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/e0/FFXIII_Characters.jpg/250px-FFXIII_Characters.jpg" height="333" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="250"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="FFXIII Characters" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="FFXIII_Characters.jpg" data-image-name="FFXIII Characters.jpg" height="333" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20111031122945/finalfantasy/images/thumb/e/e0/FFXIII_Characters.jpg/250px-FFXIII_Characters.jpg" width="250"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:FFXIII_Characters.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            The main characters of
            <i>
             Final Fantasy XIII
            </i>
            , along with Serah.
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <i>
            Main article:
            <a href="/wiki/List_of_Final_Fantasy_XIII_Characters" title="List of Final Fantasy XIII Characters">
             List of Final Fantasy XIII Characters
            </a>
           </i>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          There are six playable characters in
          <i>
           Final Fantasy XIII
          </i>
          , and two
          <a href="/wiki/Guest" title="Guest">
           guest
          </a>
          characters. Although the game focuses on each of the playable characters equally, the majority of the story is told through the perspective of Lightning. The main playable characters are all l'Cie.
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Characters">
           Playable Characters
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit Playable Characters section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Lightning_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Lightning (Final Fantasy XIII)">
             Lightning
            </a>
           </b>
            The main protagonist. Lightning was a member of the
           <a href="/wiki/Guardian_Corps" title="Guardian Corps">
            Guardian Corps
           </a>
           in Bodhum before her life came crashing down when her sister Serah became a Pulse l'Cie. Regretting her refusal to believe Serah, Lightning volunteers to be Purged with the intention of saving her, only to be made a l'Cie like her. She is an agile fighter who makes use of a variety of
           <a href="/wiki/Gunblade_(Weapon_Type)" title="Gunblade (Weapon Type)">
            gunblades
           </a>
           , the
           <a href="/wiki/Blazefire_Saber" title="Blazefire Saber">
            Blazefire Saber
           </a>
           among them.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Snow_Villiers" title="Snow Villiers">
             Snow Villiers
            </a>
           </b>
            Leader of
           <a href="/wiki/NORA" title="NORA">
            NORA
           </a>
           , Snow Villiers is a sturdy man whose mannerisms are said to resemble that of a cowboy. He travels to the Hanging Edge to fight PSICOM and the Purge in the hopes of saving his fiance, Serah, who was imprisoned by the Pulse fal'Cie, only to share her fate as a l'Cie. Although Snow uses his fists to fight, his equipped 'weapon' is a runed coat, designed to enhance the wearer's strength.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Oerba_Dia_Vanille" title="Oerba Dia Vanille">
             Oerba Dia Vanille
            </a>
           </b>
            A young and spirited girl with a mysterious past who carries a heavy burden the others are initially unaware of. Getting through the events of the Purge, she tags along with Hope and finds herself wrapped up in the events leading to her joining the others. She acts as the narrator of the story and can be considered a deuteragonist. Her weapon of choice is called the Binding Rod.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Sazh_Katzroy" title="Sazh Katzroy">
             Sazh Katzroy
            </a>
           </b>
            A middle-aged man with dark skin and an afro. He was formerly in the military, but now works as a civilian airship pilot. In the hopes of saving his son, Dajh, he boards the Purge train to the Hanging Edge, only to become a l'Cie himself. He owns a
           <a href="/wiki/Chocobo_Chick" title="Chocobo Chick">
            Chocobo Chick
           </a>
           that hides in his hair. He fights with two pistols that can be combined into a rifle.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Hope_Estheim" title="Hope Estheim">
             Hope Estheim
            </a>
           </b>
            A young boy who, along with his mother, is part of the group of exiles onboard the Purge train. During an unsuccessful resistance effort by NORA, his mother dies in the conflict. Blaming Snow for his mother's death, Hope follows him but ends up becoming a l'Cie and being forced to work with him and the others as he waits for his chance to get revenge. He wields boomerangs in battle.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Oerba_Yun_Fang" title="Oerba Yun Fang">
             Oerba Yun Fang
            </a>
           </b>
            A wild-looking woman with a large tattoo on one arm and a scorched mark of the l'Cie on the other. She first appears with Cid Raines and the Cavalry with the intention of capturing Snow in Lake Bresha. However, she has a more complicated agenda, as she searches for a friend and aims to complete her Focus. Spears are her weapon of choice.
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Guests">
           Guests
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit Guests section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Gadot" title="Gadot">
             Gadot
            </a>
           </b>
            A member of NORA and Snow's childhood friend. He is a dark-skinned man with orange hair and teal clothes. His design is based on NBA and hip hop fashion. He uses a machine gun in battle.
          </li>
          <li>
           <b>
            <a href="/wiki/Lebreau" title="Lebreau">
             Lebreau
            </a>
           </b>
            A woman with black hair and a butterfly tattoo on her shoulder. She is the only female member of NORA. Her outfit is based on volleyball players, wearing short shorts and a tank top-like shirt with puffy sleeves. She uses a rifle in battle.
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Story">

            </i>

          <h3>
           <span class="mw-headline" id="Fates_Intertwined">
            Fates Intertwined
           </span>
           <span class="editsection">
            <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit Fates Intertwined section">
             <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
             Edit
            </a>
           </span>
          </h3>
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <i>
             See also:
             <a href="/wiki/Datalog/The_Thirteen_Days" title="Datalog/The Thirteen Days">
              Datalog/The Thirteen Days
             </a>
             and
             <a href="/wiki/Datalog/Events" title="Datalog/Events">
              Datalog/Events
             </a>
            </i>
           </dd>
          </dl>
          <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
           <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130605215403/finalfantasy/images/6/6c/Bodhum_Purge.png">
            <img alt="Bodhum Purge" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Bodhum_Purge.png" data-image-name="Bodhum Purge.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130605215403/finalfantasy/images/thumb/6/6c/Bodhum_Purge.png/180px-Bodhum_Purge.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Bodhum Purge" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Bodhum_Purge.png" data-image-name="Bodhum Purge.png" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130605215403/finalfantasy/images/thumb/6/6c/Bodhum_Purge.png/180px-Bodhum_Purge.png" width="180"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <figcaption>
            <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Bodhum_Purge.png">
            </a>
            <p class="caption">
             The PSICOM army Purges the town of Bodhum.
            </p>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           Having been secluded from the outside world for so long, the citizens of Cocoon have become paranoid of Gran Pulse. The
           <a href="/wiki/Sanctum_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Sanctum (Final Fantasy XIII)">
            Sanctum
           </a>
           , Cocoon's government, led by the fal'Cie
           <a href="/wiki/Eden_(Fal%27Cie)" title="Eden (Fal'Cie)">
            Eden
           </a>
           and
           <a href="/wiki/Primarch" title="Primarch">
            Primarch
           </a>
           <a href="/wiki/Galenth_Dysley" title="Galenth Dysley">
            Galenth Dysley
           </a>
           , have issued an edict whereupon any individuals suspected to have come in contact with anyone or anything from the lowerworld are to be banished from Cocoon.
          </p>
          <p>
           One day there was an incident at the
           <a href="/wiki/Euride_Gorge" title="Euride Gorge">
            Euride Gorge
           </a>
           Energy Plant believed to have been caused by Pulse l'Cie. L'Cie are servants of the fal'Cie who branded them, compelled to carry out the Focus given to them by the deity, as the punishment for defying it is cruel: be turned into a mindless monster known as a
           <a href="/wiki/Cie%27th" title="Cie'th">
            Cie'th
           </a>
           . Six days later, a Pulse fal'Cie was discovered in an ancient Pulsian relic near the seaside town of
           <a href="/wiki/Bodhum" title="Bodhum">
            Bodhum
           </a>
           . Mass panic broke out and soon Cocoon's citizens were crying out for the expulsion of the entire town to Pulse, prompting the Sanctum to initiate the
           <a href="/wiki/Purge" title="Purge">
            Purge
           </a>
           . Within the next two days the Sanctum's personal army,
           <a href="/wiki/PSICOM" title="PSICOM">
            PSICOM
           </a>
           , quarantined Bodhum, seized the town's inhabitants regardless of whether they are citizens or tourists, and forced them onto Purge trains. The people were taken to the restricted
           <a href="/wiki/Hanging_Edge" title="Hanging Edge">
            Hanging Edge
           </a>
           zone, along with the Pulse fal'Cie,
           <a href="/wiki/Anima_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Anima (Final Fantasy XIII)">
            Anima
           </a>
           , contained within the relic, known as the
           <a href="/wiki/Pulse_Vestige" title="Pulse Vestige">
            Pulse Vestige
           </a>
           .
          </p>
          <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
           <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img4.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110826044044/finalfantasy/images/f/f4/HangingEdge.jpg">
            <img alt="HangingEdge" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="HangingEdge.jpg" data-image-name="HangingEdge.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110826044044/finalfantasy/images/thumb/f/f4/HangingEdge.jpg/180px-HangingEdge.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="HangingEdge" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="HangingEdge.jpg" data-image-name="HangingEdge.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110826044044/finalfantasy/images/thumb/f/f4/HangingEdge.jpg/180px-HangingEdge.jpg" width="180"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <figcaption>
            <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:HangingEdge.jpg">
            </a>
            <p class="caption">
             The Purge train enters the Hanging Edge.
            </p>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           One of the many onboard a Purge train is Lightning, a former Guardian Corps soldier who seeks to reach Anima and save her sister, Serah Farron. Ten days prior Serah had accidentally come into contact with the fal'Cie and become a Pulse l'Cie, and is now being held captive by Anima in the Pulse Vestige. Accompanying her is Sazh Katzroy, a civilian
           <a href="/wiki/Airship_(Term)" title="Airship (Term)">
            airship
           </a>
           pilot with a secret reason for pursuing the fal'Cie. They stop the train and fight their way through the Hanging Edge as the Purge's true nature is revealed: instead of a forced migration to Gran Pulse as the Sanctum had everyone believe, it is a genocide. Elsewhere, Snow Villiers and his friends in the rebel group NORA rally the deportees in a rebellion against PSICOM as he is also trying to rescue Serah, as she is his fiance. Two youths caught up in the chaos, Hope Estheim and Vanille, become involved when Hope's mother,
           <a href="/wiki/Nora_Estheim" title="Nora Estheim">
            Nora Estheim
           </a>
           , joins Snow's resistance army and dies under his care, prompting the two to pursue him.
          </p>
          <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
           <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013152040/finalfantasy/images/f/f3/Serah_crystallize.png">
            <img alt="Serah crystallize" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Serah_crystallize.png" data-image-name="Serah crystallize.png" data-src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013152040/finalfantasy/images/thumb/f/f3/Serah_crystallize.png/180px-Serah_crystallize.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Serah crystallize" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Serah_crystallize.png" data-image-name="Serah crystallize.png" height="101" src="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141013152040/finalfantasy/images/thumb/f/f3/Serah_crystallize.png/180px-Serah_crystallize.png" width="180"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <figcaption>
            <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Serah_crystallize.png">
            </a>
            <p class="caption">
             Serah enters a crystal sleep.
            </p>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           The five come together in the Pulse Vestige where they find Serah. She urges Lightning to save Cocoon before entering
           <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Stasis" title="Crystal Stasis">
            crystal stasis
           </a>
           , a crystal sleep a l'Cie enters upon fulfilling their Focus. Lightning believes Serah is dead, while Snow refuses to give up the hope she will awaken someday. Seeking vengeance on Anima, Lightning heads into Anima's Throne to destroy the fal'Cie responsible for Serah's fate.
          </p>
          <p>
           As the party faces Anima, PSICOM forces blast the Pulse Vestige and everything in it to pieces. The party is transported into an otherworldly realm where the god Pulse transforms Lightning and her companions into l'Cie, showing them a dreamlike vision of their Focus involving the capital city of
           <a href="/wiki/Eden_(Location)" title="Eden (Location)">
            Eden
           </a>
           and Ragnarok. They fall down towards
           <a href="/wiki/Lake_Bresha" title="Lake Bresha">
            Lake Bresha
           </a>
           below but survive due to Anima crystallizing the area in its death throes.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <span class="mw-headline" id="Separate_Paths">
            Separate Paths
           </span>
           <span class="editsection">
            <a href="/wiki/Final_Fantasy_XIII?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit Separate Paths section">
             <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
             Edit
            </a>
           </span>
          </h3>
          <p>
           Now enemies of the state, the newly branded l'Cie assume their Focus is to destroy Cocoon although Snow believes it to be Serah's wish to save it. They set off to escape the lake and come across Serah's crystallized form that has become part of the crystallized lake. Snow insists on staying by Serah's side while the others seek to outrun pursuit as PSICOM is hunting them and other Purge survivors. The party splits with Snow staying to dig out Serah, while Lightning and rest head to the ruins of an old city at the lake's edge where they come across an airship left by a PSICOM patrol.
          </p>
          <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
           <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130810012703/finalfantasy/images/1/17/Snow_Shivas.jpg">
            <img alt="Snow Shivas" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Snow_Shivas.jpg" data-image-name="Snow Shivas.jpg" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130810012703/finalfantasy/images/thumb/1/17/Snow_Shivas.jpg/180px-Snow_Shivas.jpg" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Snow Shivas" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Snow_Shivas.jpg" data-image-name="Snow Shivas.jpg" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20130810012703/finalfantasy/images/thumb/1/17/Snow_Shivas.jpg/180px-Snow_Shivas.jpg" width="180"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <figcaption>
            <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Snow_Shivas.jpg">
            </a>
            <p class="caption">
             Snow and the Shiva Sisters.
            </p>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           After nearly being killed by a PSICOM platoon sent to exterminate him, the
           <a href="/wiki/Shiva#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Shiva">
            Shiva Sisters
           </a>
           manifest in front of Snow and after subduing them he receives his
           <a href="/wiki/Eidolon_(Final_Fantasy_XIII)" title="Eidolon (Final Fantasy XIII)">
            Eidolon
           </a>
           , mysterious otherworldly beings only l'Cie can tame. He is captured along with Serah's crystal by another Pulse l'Cie,
           <a href="/wiki/Oerba_Yun_Fang" title="Oerba Yun Fang">
            Oerba Yun Fang
           </a>
           , as well as
           <a href="/wiki/Rygdea" title="Rygdea">
            Rygdea
           </a>
           and other members of the
           <a href="/wiki/Cavalry" title="Cavalry">
            Cavalry
           </a>
           , a division of the Guardian Corps.
          </p>
          <p>
           Sazh pilots the stolen airship through the blockade and while onboard the group views a live newscast interviewing Galenth Dysley about the ongoing operation being carried out by PSICOM after the "success" of the Purge. The airship is shot down by PSICOM pursuit and crashes in the
           <a href="/wiki/Vile_Peaks" title="Vile Peaks">
            Vile Peaks
           </a>
           . The party splits after a disagreement on their Focus: Sazh and Vanille wish to flee from their pursuers, but Lightning is intent on getting revenge by destroying the Sanctum and the fal'Cie Eden said to be in control of it. Accompanied by Hope, she intends to travel through the
           <a href="/wiki/Gapra_Whitewood" title="Gapra Whitewood">
            Gapra Whitewood
           </a>
           , his hometown of
           <a href="/wiki/Palumpolum" title="Palumpolum">
            Palumpolum
           </a>
           , and take a train to Eden, the heart of the Sanctum government.
          </p>
          <p>
           As she and Hope trek through the remainder of the Vile Peaks the pressure of keeping Hope safe and dealing with the enemy soldiers take their toll on Lightning and she snaps at him for being unable to keep up with her. The Eidolon
           <a href="/wiki/Odin#Final_Fantasy_XIII" title="Odin">
            Odin
           </a>
           appears and attacks Hope as if to force her to choose between her mission and him. Together they bring the Eidolon under control, and Lightning resolves to help Hope toughen up as they continue on their mission together.
          </p>
          <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
           <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://img1.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141011194016/finalfantasy/images/7/7f/Hope_blames_Snow.png">
            <img alt="Hope blames Snow" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Hope_blames_Snow.png" data-image-name="Hope blames Snow.png" data-src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141011194016/finalfantasy/images/thumb/7/7f/Hope_blames_Snow.png/180px-Hope_blames_Snow.png" height="101" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Hope blames Snow" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Hope_blames_Snow.png" data-image-name="Hope blames Snow.png" height="101" src="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20141011194016/finalfantasy/images/thumb/7/7f/Hope_blames_Snow.png/180px-Hope_blames_Snow.png" width="180"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <figcaption>
            <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Hope_blames_Snow.png">
            </a>
            <p class="caption">
             Lightning and Hope in the Gapra Whitewood.
            </p>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
          <p>
           Snow and Serah's crystal are taken aboard the Cavalry's headquarters, the airship
           <i>
